
The parity check matrix for the dual of W(3,19) minus a spread is a 19b x 
20b matrix, where b is 362.

The 1 coordinates of the first row of the circulants in the qx(q+1) rep matrix is given by \
Hrep.

The length of the code is 7240 and the check matrix has rank 
3801, so the full code has dimension 3439.

There is a generator matrix for the subcode of the form (P | id) where P is quasi cyclic 
9b x 11b matrix, whose first rows are in the matrix Pbin.

The subcode has dimension 3258 so the rate is 0.45.
